[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The region was originally allocated via `xmlFuzzMalloc` → `xmlStrndup` → [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer-enabled LibFuzzer run against libxml2’s API fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`api`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreported a double-free in `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`. The backtrace shows that a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomment node’s content is freed twice: once during processing in `api.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3580[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and again during teardown. To work around this, a patch was attempted in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tree.c` that removes the content free for comment nodes by introducing a new [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhelper [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlFreeComment`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and nulling out `cur->content`. The patch, however, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclared `xmlFreeComment` inside another function, leading to a compiler error [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m“function definition is not allowed here”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and an unused-parameter warning. As a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresult, the build failed and the fuzzer could not be rebuilt.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A fuzzing run [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`run_fuzzer api -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m …`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggers an AddressSanitizer error: [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  “ERROR: AddressSanitizer: attempting double-free on [0m[1;36m0x5020000000b0[0m[39m in thread T0” [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The first free happens in `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` at `fuzz/api.[0m[1;92mc:3580[0m[39m`.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory was originally allocated by `xmlFuzzMalloc` → `xmlStrndup` → [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlNewComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `xmlNewComment` in `tree.[0m[1;92mc:2583[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- On exit, the comment node’s destructor or cleanup code frees `cur->content` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magain, causing the second free.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The summary line points at `api.[0m[1;92mc:3580:9[0m[39m` in `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` as the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediate location of the double free.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The issue arises inside the fuzzer harness but reflects a memory-management [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmismatch in libxml2’s comment-node handling.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allocation chain: xmlFuzzMalloc → xmlStrndup → xmlNewComment.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Two separate code paths free the same pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`cur->content`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- File modified: `tree.c` around the definition of `xmlNewComment`.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removed the original assignments:  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `cur->name = xmlStringComment;`  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `cur->content = [0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Introduced a new function, `[0m[1;35mxmlFreeComment[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlNodePtr cur[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, intended to null out[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`cur->content` before freeing the node to prevent the double free.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code snippet from patch:  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```diff[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
